Fixed `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` to read schema files through `_read_utf8_text_file()`, added missing-docs CLI regression coverage in `tests/test_claude_goal.py`, and hardened `tests/test_claude_goal.py` plus `tests/test_install_goal.py` subprocess decoding with UTF-8/error replacement for Korean Windows paths. |

Focused regression pytest passed (`1 passed, 119 deselected`); schema cluster passed (`5 passed, 115 deselected`); cp949 helper regression passed (`1 passed, 119 deselected`); full `tests/test_claude_goal.py` passed (`120 passed`); installer decoding focused pytest passed (`3 passed, 18 deselected`); final full isolated pytest passed (`174 passed`). Continued the `/goal` reproduce -> isolate -> root-cause -> fix -> verify loop in the separate `claude-goal/` repo on branch `improve/goal-system`, preserving existing nested WIP plus the already-recorded T-1761 inline flag-like value-option surface, T-1760 invoke split-form value-option flag-consumption surface, and T-1759 direct boolean explicit-value surface. | Work | **T-1798 claude-goal installer option-before-positionals regression fix**. Continued the `/goal` reproduce -> isolate -> root-cause -> fix -> verify loop in the separate `claude-goal/` repo on branch `improve/goal-system`, preserving existing nested WIP plus concurrently recorded T-1797/T-1796 and root auto-research dirty-handoff work. Direct installer CLI probing after T-1797 exposed that the new option prevalidation still treated a boolean flag followed by a positional path as a flag value: `python goal/scripts/install_goal.py --no-backup <settings> <script>` needed to be accepted as normal argparse option-before-positionals usage, while `<settings> <script> --no-backup false` still needed the T-1795 `--no-backup does not accept a value` diagnostic. Classification: functional error plus loading/feedback copy. External reference checked: Python argparse documents option parsing by prefix and has a separate `parse_intermixed_args()` API for option/positional intermixing, so this installer should support options before all positionals without pretending to support arbitrary intermixing. Root cause: `prevalidate_option_values()` lacked positional context and rejected any non-option token after a boolean option. Fixed `goal/scripts/install_goal.py` so boolean split-value validation is positional-count aware: `--restore-backup` may precede the settings path, `--no-backup` may precede the install positionals, and `--yes` may precede the restore settings path, while post-positional extra values still get flag-specific errors. Added tests in `tests/test_install_goal.py` for valid option-before-positionals install/restore and retained the original boolean-value rejection cases. |
| Next Priorities | Verification passed in `claude-goal/`: direct after-fix probes confirm `--no-backup <settings> <script>` installs successfully and `<settings> <script> --no-backup false`, `<settings> --restore-backup false`, and `<settings> --restore-backup --yes false` still exit `2` with flag-specific value errors. Focused parser/install pytest passed (`11 passed, 53 deselected` with repo-local `--basetemp`), full installer module passed with exported `PYTHONUTF8=1` (`64 passed`), and full isolated pytest with exported `PYTHONUTF8=1` passed (`256 passed`). Root cause: both CLI entrypoints only set `errors=backslashreplace` on stdout/stderr while leaving the child process output encoding on the Windows locale, but the test harness and CI-style captures decode as UTF-8. Continued the `/goal` CLI UX loop in the separate `claude-goal/` repo, preserving existing nested WIP plus concurrent root auto-research relay work.
